\DoxyCodeLine{00035\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00036\ \textcolor{comment}{/*TEXT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00037\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00038\ \textcolor{comment}{pigpio\ is\ a\ C\ library\ for\ the\ Raspberry\ which\ allows\ control\ of\ the\ GPIO.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00039\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00040\ \textcolor{comment}{*Features*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00041\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00042\ \textcolor{comment}{o\ hardware\ timed\ PWM\ on\ any\ of\ GPIO\ 0-\/31}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00043\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00044\ \textcolor{comment}{o\ hardware\ timed\ servo\ pulses\ on\ any\ of\ GPIO\ 0-\/31}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00045\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00046\ \textcolor{comment}{o\ callbacks\ when\ any\ of\ GPIO\ 0-\/31\ change\ state}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00047\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00048\ \textcolor{comment}{o\ callbacks\ at\ timed\ intervals}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00049\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00050\ \textcolor{comment}{o\ reading/writing\ all\ of\ the\ GPIO\ in\ a\ bank\ as\ one\ operation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00051\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00052\ \textcolor{comment}{o\ individually\ setting\ GPIO\ modes,\ reading\ and\ writing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00053\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00054\ \textcolor{comment}{o\ notifications\ when\ any\ of\ GPIO\ 0-\/31\ change\ state}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00055\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00056\ \textcolor{comment}{o\ the\ construction\ of\ output\ waveforms\ with\ microsecond\ timing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00057\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00058\ \textcolor{comment}{o\ rudimentary\ permission\ control\ over\ GPIO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00059\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00060\ \textcolor{comment}{o\ a\ simple\ interface\ to\ start\ and\ stop\ new\ threads}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00061\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00062\ \textcolor{comment}{o\ I2C,\ SPI,\ and\ serial\ link\ wrappers}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00063\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00064\ \textcolor{comment}{o\ creating\ and\ running\ scripts}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00065\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00066\ \textcolor{comment}{*GPIO*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00067\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00068\ \textcolor{comment}{ALL\ GPIO\ are\ identified\ by\ their\ Broadcom\ number.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00069\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00070\ \textcolor{comment}{*Credits*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00071\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00072\ \textcolor{comment}{The\ PWM\ and\ servo\ pulses\ are\ timed\ using\ the\ DMA\ and\ PWM\ peripherals.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00073\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00074\ \textcolor{comment}{This\ use\ was\ inspired\ by\ Richard\ Hirst's\ servoblaster\ kernel\ module.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00075\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00076\ \textcolor{comment}{*Usage*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00077\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00078\ \textcolor{comment}{Include\ <pigpio.h>\ in\ your\ source\ files.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00079\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00080\ \textcolor{comment}{Assuming\ your\ source\ is\ in\ prog.c\ use\ the\ following\ command\ to\ build\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00081\ \textcolor{comment}{run\ the\ executable.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00082\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00083\ \textcolor{comment}{.\ .}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00084\ \textcolor{comment}{gcc\ -\/Wall\ -\/pthread\ -\/o\ prog\ prog.c\ -\/lpigpio\ -\/lrt}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00085\ \textcolor{comment}{sudo\ ./prog}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00086\ \textcolor{comment}{.\ .}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00087\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00088\ \textcolor{comment}{For\ examples\ of\ usage\ see\ the\ C\ programs\ within\ the\ pigpio\ archive\ file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00089\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00090\ \textcolor{comment}{*Notes*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00091\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00092\ \textcolor{comment}{All\ the\ functions\ which\ return\ an\ int\ return\ <\ 0\ on\ error.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00093\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00094\ \textcolor{comment}{[*gpioInitialise*]\ must\ be\ called\ before\ all\ other\ library\ functions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00095\ \textcolor{comment}{with\ the\ following\ exceptions:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00096\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00097\ \textcolor{comment}{.\ .}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00098\ \textcolor{comment}{[*gpioCfg**]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00099\ \textcolor{comment}{[*gpioVersion*]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00100\ \textcolor{comment}{[*gpioHardwareRevision*]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00101\ \textcolor{comment}{.\ .}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00102\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00103\ \textcolor{comment}{If\ the\ library\ is\ not\ initialised\ all\ but\ the\ [*gpioCfg**],}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00104\ \textcolor{comment}{[*gpioVersion*],\ and\ [*gpioHardwareRevision*]\ functions\ will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00105\ \textcolor{comment}{return\ error\ PI\_NOT\_INITIALISED.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00106\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00107\ \textcolor{comment}{If\ the\ library\ is\ initialised\ the\ [*gpioCfg**]\ functions\ will\ return}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00108\ \textcolor{comment}{error\ PI\_INITIALISED.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00109\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00110\ \textcolor{comment}{If\ you\ intend\ to\ rely\ on\ signals\ sent\ to\ your\ application,\ you\ should}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00111\ \textcolor{comment}{turn\ off\ the\ internal\ signal\ handling\ as\ shown\ in\ this\ example:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00112\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00113\ \textcolor{comment}{.\ .}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00114\ \textcolor{comment}{int\ cfg\ =\ gpioCfgGetInternals();}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00115\ \textcolor{comment}{cfg\ |=\ PI\_CFG\_NOSIGHANDLER;\ \ //\ (1<<10)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00116\ \textcolor{comment}{gpioCfgSetInternals(cfg);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00117\ \textcolor{comment}{int\ status\ =\ gpioInitialise();}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00118\ \textcolor{comment}{.\ .}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00119\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00120\ \textcolor{comment}{TEXT*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00121\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{01558\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ WARNING:\ this\ wraps\ around\ from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01559\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 4294967295\ to\ 0\ roughly\ every\ 72\ minutes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01560\ \textcolor{comment}{.\ .}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01561\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01562\ \textcolor{comment}{The\ underlying\ Linux\ sysfs\ GPIO\ interface\ is\ used\ to\ provide}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01563\ \textcolor{comment}{the\ interrupt\ services.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01564\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01565\ \textcolor{comment}{The\ first\ time\ the\ function\ is\ called,\ with\ a\ non-\/NULL\ f,\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01566\ \textcolor{comment}{GPIO\ is\ exported,\ set\ to\ be\ an\ input,\ and\ set\ to\ interrupt}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01567\ \textcolor{comment}{on\ the\ given\ edge\ and\ timeout.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01568\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01569\ \textcolor{comment}{Subsequent\ calls,\ with\ a\ non-\/NULL\ f,\ can\ vary\ one\ or\ more\ of\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01570\ \textcolor{comment}{edge,\ timeout,\ or\ function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01571\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01572\ \textcolor{comment}{The\ ISR\ may\ be\ cancelled\ by\ passing\ a\ NULL\ f,\ in\ which\ case\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01573\ \textcolor{comment}{GPIO\ is\ unexported.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01574\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01575\ \textcolor{comment}{The\ tick\ is\ that\ read\ at\ the\ time\ the\ process\ was\ informed\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01576\ \textcolor{comment}{the\ interrupt.\ \ This\ will\ be\ a\ variable\ number\ of\ microseconds}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01577\ \textcolor{comment}{after\ the\ interrupt\ occurred.\ \ Typically\ the\ latency\ will\ be\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01578\ \textcolor{comment}{the\ order\ of\ 50\ microseconds.\ \ The\ latency\ is\ not\ guaranteed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01579\ \textcolor{comment}{and\ will\ vary\ with\ system\ load.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01580\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01581\ \textcolor{comment}{The\ level\ is\ that\ read\ at\ the\ time\ the\ process\ was\ informed\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01582\ \textcolor{comment}{the\ interrupt,\ or\ PI\_TIMEOUT\ if\ the\ optional\ interrupt\ timeout}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01583\ \textcolor{comment}{expired.\ \ It\ may\ not\ be\ the\ same\ as\ the\ expected\ edge\ as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01584\ \textcolor{comment}{interrupts\ happening\ in\ rapid\ succession\ may\ be\ missed\ by\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01585\ \textcolor{comment}{kernel\ (i.e.\ this\ mechanism\ can\ not\ be\ used\ to\ capture\ several}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01586\ \textcolor{comment}{interrupts\ only\ a\ few\ microseconds\ apart).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01587\ \textcolor{comment}{D*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01588\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{01731\ \textcolor{comment}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01949\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{pigpio_8h_af39b648323a7d3afd27de5492ec7aa99}{gpioWaveCreate}}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{void});}
\DoxyCodeLine{01950\ \textcolor{comment}{/*D}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01951\ \textcolor{comment}{This\ function\ creates\ a\ waveform\ from\ the\ data\ provided\ by\ the\ prior}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01952\ \textcolor{comment}{calls\ to\ the\ [*gpioWaveAdd**]\ functions.\ \ Upon\ success\ a\ wave\ id}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01953\ \textcolor{comment}{greater\ than\ or\ equal\ to\ 0\ is\ returned,\ otherwise\ PI\_EMPTY\_WAVEFORM,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01954\ \textcolor{comment}{PI\_TOO\_MANY\_CBS,\ PI\_TOO\_MANY\_OOL,\ or\ PI\_NO\_WAVEFORM\_ID.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01955\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01956\ \textcolor{comment}{The\ data\ provided\ by\ the\ [*gpioWaveAdd**]\ functions\ is\ consumed\ by\ this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01957\ \textcolor{comment}{function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01958\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01959\ \textcolor{comment}{As\ many\ waveforms\ may\ be\ created\ as\ there\ is\ space\ available.\ \ The}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01960\ \textcolor{comment}{wave\ id\ is\ passed\ to\ [*gpioWaveTxSend*]\ to\ specify\ the\ waveform\ to\ transmit.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01961\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01962\ \textcolor{comment}{Normal\ usage\ would\ be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01963\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01964\ \textcolor{comment}{Step\ 1.\ [*gpioWaveClear*]\ to\ clear\ all\ waveforms\ and\ added\ data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01965\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01966\ \textcolor{comment}{Step\ 2.\ [*gpioWaveAdd**]\ calls\ to\ supply\ the\ waveform\ data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01967\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01968\ \textcolor{comment}{Step\ 3.\ [*gpioWaveCreate*]\ to\ create\ the\ waveform\ and\ get\ a\ unique\ id}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01969\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01970\ \textcolor{comment}{Repeat\ steps\ 2\ and\ 3\ as\ needed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01971\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01972\ \textcolor{comment}{Step\ 4.\ [*gpioWaveTxSend*]\ with\ the\ id\ of\ the\ waveform\ to\ transmit.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01973\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01974\ \textcolor{comment}{A\ waveform\ comprises\ one\ of\ more\ pulses.\ \ Each\ pulse\ consists\ of\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01975\ \textcolor{comment}{[*gpioPulse\_t*]\ structure.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01976\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01977\ \textcolor{comment}{.\ .}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01978\ \textcolor{comment}{typedef\ struct}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01979\ \textcolor{comment}{\{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01980\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ uint32\_t\ gpioOn;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01981\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ uint32\_t\ gpioOff;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01982\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ uint32\_t\ usDelay;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01983\ \textcolor{comment}{\}\ gpioPulse\_t;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01984\ \textcolor{comment}{.\ .}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01985\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01986\ \textcolor{comment}{The\ fields\ specify}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01987\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01988\ \textcolor{comment}{1)\ the\ GPIO\ to\ be\ switched\ on\ at\ the\ start\ of\ the\ pulse.\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{01989\ \textcolor{comment}{2)\ the\ GPIO\ to\ be\ switched\ off\ at\ the\ start\ of\ the\ pulse.\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{01990\ \textcolor{comment}{3)\ the\ delay\ in\ microseconds\ before\ the\ next\ pulse.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01991\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01992\ \textcolor{comment}{Any\ or\ all\ the\ fields\ can\ be\ zero.\ \ It\ doesn't\ make\ any\ sense\ to}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01994\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01995\ \textcolor{comment}{When\ a\ waveform\ is\ started\ each\ pulse\ is\ executed\ in\ order\ with\ the}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01997\ \textcolor{comment}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02096\ \textcolor{comment}{/*D}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02098\ \textcolor{comment}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02115\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02116\ \textcolor{comment}{A\ blocks\ of\ waves\ may\ be\ transmitted\ multiple\ times\ by\ using}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02117\ \textcolor{comment}{the\ loop\ commands.\ The\ block\ is\ bracketed\ by\ loop\ start\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02118\ \textcolor{comment}{end\ commands.\ \ Loops\ may\ be\ nested.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02119\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02120\ \textcolor{comment}{Delays\ between\ waves\ may\ be\ added\ with\ the\ delay\ command.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02121\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02122\ \textcolor{comment}{The\ following\ command\ codes\ are\ supported:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02123\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02124\ \textcolor{comment}{Name\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ @\ Cmd\ \&\ Data\ @\ Meaning}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02125\ \textcolor{comment}{Loop\ Start\ \ \ @\ 255\ 0\ \ \ \ \ \ @\ Identify\ start\ of\ a\ wave\ block}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02126\ \textcolor{comment}{Loop\ Repeat\ \ @\ 255\ 1\ x\ y\ \ @\ loop\ x\ +\ y*256\ times}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02127\ \textcolor{comment}{Delay\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ @\ 255\ 2\ x\ y\ \ @\ delay\ x\ +\ y*256\ microseconds}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02128\ \textcolor{comment}{Loop\ Forever\ @\ 255\ 3\ \ \ \ \ \ @\ loop\ forever}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02129\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02130\ \textcolor{comment}{If\ present\ Loop\ Forever\ must\ be\ the\ last\ entry\ in\ the\ chain.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02131\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02132\ \textcolor{comment}{The\ code\ is\ currently\ dimensioned\ to\ support\ a\ chain\ with\ roughly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02133\ \textcolor{comment}{600\ entries\ and\ 20\ loop\ counters.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02969\ \textcolor{comment}{/*D}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02970\ \textcolor{comment}{This\ function\ provides\ a\ low-\/level\ interface\ to\ the\ SPI/I2C\ Slave}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02971\ \textcolor{comment}{peripheral\ on\ the\ BCM\ chip.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02972\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02973\ \textcolor{comment}{This\ peripheral\ allows\ the\ Pi\ to\ act\ as\ a\ hardware\ slave\ device}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02974\ \textcolor{comment}{on\ an\ I2C\ or\ SPI\ bus.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02975\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02976\ \textcolor{comment}{This\ is\ not\ a\ bit\ bang\ version\ and\ as\ such\ is\ OS\ timing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02977\ \textcolor{comment}{independent.\ The\ bus\ timing\ is\ handled\ directly\ by\ the\ chip.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02978\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02979\ \textcolor{comment}{The\ output\ process\ is\ simple.\ You\ simply\ append\ data\ to\ the\ FIFO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02980\ \textcolor{comment}{buffer\ on\ the\ chip.\ \ This\ works\ like\ a\ queue,\ you\ add\ data\ to\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02981\ \textcolor{comment}{queue\ and\ the\ master\ removes\ it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02982\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02983\ \textcolor{comment}{The\ function\ sets\ the\ BSC\ mode,\ writes\ any\ data\ in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02984\ \textcolor{comment}{the\ transmit\ buffer\ to\ the\ BSC\ transmit\ FIFO,\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02985\ \textcolor{comment}{copies\ any\ data\ in\ the\ BSC\ receive\ FIFO\ to\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02986\ \textcolor{comment}{receive\ buffer.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{04872\ \textcolor{comment}{A\ full\ channel\ only\ requires\ one\ DMA\ control\ block\ regardless\ of\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04873\ \textcolor{comment}{length\ of\ a\ pulse\ delay.\ \ Channels\ 7\ to\ 14\ (lite\ channels)\ require}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04874\ \textcolor{comment}{one\ DMA\ control\ block\ for\ each\ 16383\ microseconds\ of\ delay.\ \ I.e.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04875\ \textcolor{comment}{a\ 10\ second\ pulse\ delay\ requires\ one\ control\ block\ on\ a\ full\ channel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04876\ \textcolor{comment}{and\ 611\ control\ blocks\ on\ a\ lite\ channel.}}
